Nickel index of the Feynman diagram: e12|e3|33||:0B_bV_vV|0b_bv|vV_vv|| 

Diagram symmetry factor: 1 

Diagram description start.

Propagators (lines) in the diagram: 
{'line 0': [(0, 1), ['b', 'V']], 'line 1': [(0, 2), ['v', 'V']], 'line 2': [(1, 3), ['b', 'v']], 'line 3': [(2, 3), ['v', 'V']], 'line 4': [(2, 3), ['v', 'v']]} 
Notation for line n: [(vertex_1, vertex_2), (field_flows_out_of_vertex_1, field_flows_into_vertex_2)]

Loops in the diagram for a given internal momentum: 
[('line 3', 'line 4'), ('line 0', 'line 1', 'line 2', 'line 3')] 

Momentum propagating along the lines: 
{'line 0': k, 'line 1': -k + p, 'line 2': k, 'line 3': -k + p - q, 'line 4': q}

Frequency propagating along the lines: 
{'line 0': w_k, 'line 1': w - w_k, 'line 2': w_k, 'line 3': w - w_k - w_q, 'line 4': w_q}

Diagram integrand: 
PbV(k, w_k, 1, 4)*Pbv_scalar_part(k, w_k, 5, 9)*PvV(-k, -w_k, 2, 6)*PvV(-k - q, -w_k - w_q, 7, 10)*Pvv(q, w_q, 8, 11)*vertex_factor_Bbv(p, 0, 1, 2)*vertex_factor_Vbb(k, 4, 3, 5)*vertex_factor_Vvv(-k, 6, 7, 8)*vertex_factor_Vvv(-k - q, 10, 9, 11)

The calculation of the integrand is divided into two stages: 
1. The calculation of the tensor structure T_ij 
2. The calculation of the scalar part F 
See file General_notation.txt for details.

Expression for the scalar function F: 
-A**2*D_v(k)*D_v(q)*beta(nuo, k, w_k)**2*beta(nuo, q, w_q)*beta(nuo, k + q, w_k + w_q)*beta_star(nuo, q, w_q)*sc_prod(B, k)**2/(xi(k, w_k)**2*xi(q, w_q)*xi(k + q, w_k + w_q)*xi_star(k, w_k)**2*xi_star(q, w_q))

Expression for the tensor function T_ij (numbers for vector indices instead of alphabetic [1]): 
-((-mom(k, 9) - mom(q, 9))*kd(10, 11) + (-mom(k, 11) - mom(q, 11))*kd(10, 9))*(kd(4, 3)*mom(k, 5) + kd(4, 5)*mom(k, 3))*(-kd(6, 7)*mom(k, 8) - kd(6, 8)*mom(k, 7))*(I*rho*H(k, 5, 9) + P(k, 5, 9))*(I*rho*H(q, 8, 11) + P(q, 8, 11))*(-A*kd(0, 2)*mom(p, 1) + kd(0, 1)*mom(p, 2))*P(k, 1, 4)*P(k, 2, 6)*P(k + q, 7, 10)

Scalar part of the propagator product  in a Wolfram Mathematica-friendly format: 
PbV[k, w_k]*PvV[-k, -w_k]*Pbv[k, w_k]*PvV[-k - q, -w_k - w_q]*Pvv[q, w_q]

The diagram is UV-convergent: 
True

Diagram description end.

Preparation for numerical integration for the integrand's scalar part consists in carrying out a replacing of variables k, q --> B*k/nuo, B*q/nuo, after which UV-convergent part of the diagram is divided into a dimensional factor C_F and a function F1 depending only on uo and integration variables k and q: F = C_F*F1.

1. In case of UV-convergent diagrams UV-convergent part is equal to F.
1. In case of UV-divergent diagrams UV-convergent part is equal to F - F(B = 0) [1].

The expression for common C_F after momentums replacing: 
4*pi**2*A**2*go**2*nuo**11*(B/nuo)**(-2*d - 4*eps + 8)/B**10 

Calculation of T_ij. 

For UV-divergent diagrams, the expression for T_ij after calculating tensor convolutions is calculated both in the case of the presence of an external field B and for B = 0. For UV-finite diagrams, there is an expression for T_ij only in the external field. 

1. Tensor structure without the presence of B field (Lambda part): 
None 

2. Tensor structure with the presence of B field (B part): 
I*k**2*rho*(A*d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - A*d*k**3*z**2 - A*d*k**3*z_k**2 + A*d*k**3 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z + A*d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - A*d*k*q**2*z**2 - A*d*k*q**2*z_k**2 + A*d*k*q**2 - 2*A*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + 2*A*k**3*z**2 + 2*A*k**3*z_k**2 - 2*A*k**3 - 4*A*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z**3 + 2*A*k**2*q*z**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 - 4*A*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 4*A*k**2*q*z + 2*A*k**2*q*z_k**2 + 2*A*k**2*q*z_q**2 - 2*A*k**2*q + 2*A*k*q**2*z**3 - 2*A*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 4*A*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q + 4*A*k*q**2*z**2 + 2*A*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 - 4*A*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 2*A*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 2*A*k*q**2*z + 4*A*k*q**2*z_k**2 + 2*A*k*q**2*z_q**2 - 4*A*k*q**2 + 2*A*q**3*z**3 - 4*A*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 2*A*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 2*A*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 2*A*q**3*z + d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - d*k**3*z**2 - d*k**3*z_k**2 + d*k**3 + 2*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 2*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 2*d*k**2*q*z + d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - d*k*q**2*z**2 - d*k*q**2*z_k**2 + d*k*q**2 - 2*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + 2*k**3*z**2 + 2*k**3*z_k**2 - 2*k**3 - 4*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 4*k**2*q*z**3 + 2*k**2*q*z**2 + 4*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 - 4*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 4*k**2*q*z + 2*k**2*q*z_k**2 + 2*k**2*q*z_q**2 - 2*k**2*q + 2*k*q**2*z**3 - 2*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 4*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q + 4*k*q**2*z**2 + 2*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 - 4*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 2*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 2*k*q**2*z + 4*k*q**2*z_k**2 + 2*k*q**2*z_q**2 - 4*k*q**2 + 2*q**3*z**3 - 4*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 2*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 2*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 2*q**3*z)*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)/(d**2*k**2 + 2*d**2*k*q*z + d**2*q**2 - 3*d*k**2 - 6*d*k*q*z - 3*d*q**2 + 2*k**2 + 4*k*q*z + 2*q**2)

The expression for T_ij in helical MHD (A = 1): 

1. Tensor structure without the presence of B field (Lambda part): 
None 

2. Tensor structure with the presence of B field (B part): 
I*k**2*rho*(2*d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - 2*d*k**3*z**2 - 2*d*k**3*z_k**2 + 2*d*k**3 + 4*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 4*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 4*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 4*d*k**2*q*z + 2*d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 2*d*k*q**2*z**2 - 2*d*k*q**2*z_k**2 + 2*d*k*q**2 - 4*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + 4*k**3*z**2 + 4*k**3*z_k**2 - 4*k**3 - 8*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 8*k**2*q*z**3 + 4*k**2*q*z**2 + 8*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 - 8*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 8*k**2*q*z + 4*k**2*q*z_k**2 + 4*k**2*q*z_q**2 - 4*k**2*q + 4*k*q**2*z**3 - 4*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 8*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q + 8*k*q**2*z**2 + 4*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 - 8*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 4*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 4*k*q**2*z + 8*k*q**2*z_k**2 + 4*k*q**2*z_q**2 - 8*k*q**2 + 4*q**3*z**3 - 8*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 4*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 4*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 4*q**3*z)*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)/(d**2*k**2 + 2*d**2*k*q*z + d**2*q**2 - 3*d*k**2 - 6*d*k*q*z - 3*d*q**2 + 2*k**2 + 4*k*q*z + 2*q**2)

Preparation for numerical integration for the integrand's tensor part consists in carrying out a replacing of variables k, q --> B*k/nuo, B*q/nuo, after which T_ij is divided into a dimensional factor C_T and a function T1_ij depending only on uo and integration variables: T_ij = C_T*T1_ij. 
For UV divergent diagrams, this procedure applies to both Lambda part of T_ij and to B part of T_ij.

The expression for T1_B_ij (B part of T_1_ij) after momentums replacing: 
k**2*(A*d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - A*d*k**3*z**2 - A*d*k**3*z_k**2 + A*d*k**3 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z + A*d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - A*d*k*q**2*z**2 - A*d*k*q**2*z_k**2 + A*d*k*q**2 - 2*A*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + 2*A*k**3*z**2 + 2*A*k**3*z_k**2 - 2*A*k**3 - 4*A*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z**3 + 2*A*k**2*q*z**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 - 4*A*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 4*A*k**2*q*z + 2*A*k**2*q*z_k**2 + 2*A*k**2*q*z_q**2 - 2*A*k**2*q + 2*A*k*q**2*z**3 - 2*A*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 4*A*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q + 4*A*k*q**2*z**2 + 2*A*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 - 4*A*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 2*A*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 2*A*k*q**2*z + 4*A*k*q**2*z_k**2 + 2*A*k*q**2*z_q**2 - 4*A*k*q**2 + 2*A*q**3*z**3 - 4*A*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 2*A*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 2*A*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 2*A*q**3*z + d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - d*k**3*z**2 - d*k**3*z_k**2 + d*k**3 + 2*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 2*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 2*d*k**2*q*z + d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - d*k*q**2*z**2 - d*k*q**2*z_k**2 + d*k*q**2 - 2*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + 2*k**3*z**2 + 2*k**3*z_k**2 - 2*k**3 - 4*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 4*k**2*q*z**3 + 2*k**2*q*z**2 + 4*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 - 4*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 4*k**2*q*z + 2*k**2*q*z_k**2 + 2*k**2*q*z_q**2 - 2*k**2*q + 2*k*q**2*z**3 - 2*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 4*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q + 4*k*q**2*z**2 + 2*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 - 4*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 2*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 2*k*q**2*z + 4*k*q**2*z_k**2 + 2*k*q**2*z_q**2 - 4*k*q**2 + 2*q**3*z**3 - 4*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 2*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 2*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 2*q**3*z)/(d**2*k**2 + 2*d**2*k*q*z + d**2*q**2 - 3*d*k**2 - 6*d*k*q*z - 3*d*q**2 + 2*k**2 + 4*k*q*z + 2*q**2) 

The expression for C_B_T after momentums replacing: 
I*B**3*rho*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)/nuo**3 

Diagram integrand calculation end.

Calculation of the final expression for the integrand. 

F = C_int*F1*T1_ij, where C_int = C_F*C_T.
Dimensional multiplier before the integrand (with symmetric coefficient), i.e. C_int: 
4*I*Pi^2*A^2*B^(-2*d - 4*eps + 1)*go^2*nuo^(2*d + 4*eps)*rho*lcs[s, 0, 3]*mom[p, s]
